msg:1. Check-in: Accommodation vehicles need to be parked in parking lot 1, and 4 shuttle buses need to be transferred to get to the check-in building. On the first day of Qingming Festival, it took a total of one hour to queue from the parking lot to the hotel entrance. It was very frustrating. The first bus queue waited for half an hour. More than a hundred people lined up. The shuttle bus can only carry about 10 people at a time. If there is any There is less luggage and less people to carry, and the frequency does not reach 2/3 minutes. The accommodation is mixed with Japanese tourists. There is no exclusive shuttle bus for hotel guests. Large luggage can be checked into the hotel room (it took almost 2 hours). Small luggage can only be carried by yourself. There are a lot of big and small bags. It is very Embarrassing, with a child in tow. When we arrived at the scenic spot, we queued up again to check in, which took about 10-15 minutes. Then we continued to queue for the scenic spot shuttle bus and waited for another 10-15 minutes. In the middle, we walked over a bridge with large and small bags, arrived at the transfer station again to wait for the shuttle bus, and finally arrived at the hotel lobby, which took a full hour. Very bad experience.
2. Room and environment: Very good. There is a small river flowing through it, which is quiet in the bustle. There will probably be more mosquitoes in summer. In early spring, mosquitoes have already flown in groups.
3. Breakfast: Western foods are all warm and cold, including fried potatoes, sausages, etc., especially fried potatoes, which are cold. Almost every Chinese dish has chili and curry. The ones without chili are scrambled eggs with tomatoes. After staying for two days, the breakfast items are the same every day.
Check-in itinerary:
Journey 1: Parking Lot-Scenic Spot Entrance;
Journey 2: Entrance to the scenic spot - transfer station 1;
Journey 3: Walk for 1 minute to transfer station 2;
Journey 4: Transfer station 2 - hotel entrance;
Journey 5: After checking in, take the shuttle bus to the accommodation building (5 minutes walk, you need to take the shuttle bus to drag your luggage)

From the shuttle bus service to the check-in arrangements are very good. Check in from the service center, take the shuttle bus to Shanshui City, walk 200 meters after getting off the bus, arrive at the Hangu Interchange Station, and take the bus to the hotel. The front desk staff will explain all the facilities and experience items, and the concierge staff will deliver them to the room throughout the process.
Recommend an itinerary:
first day...
Arrive at noon, eat handmade dumplings at Yuanbao Pavilion near Hangu Interchange Station or Cantonese-style refreshments at Jingyue Building, then transfer to the hotel for check-in.
After a short rest, you can choose the optional forest camping refreshments in the package during the hottest time in the afternoon, and relax in the cool underground here, where the temperature is 3-5¬∞C lower than that of Beijing urban area, and leisurely recuperate the tiredness of driving from the urban area for two hours.
Two hours after afternoon tea, you can come to the open-air swimming pool. The temperature is right at this time, and the water temperature of the swimming pool is more comfortable after a day of direct sunlight.
In the evening, walk from Hangu Station to the snack street or a restaurant such as a barbecue restaurant closer to the Great Wall. Take the night tour cable car at 8 o'clock. When you arrive at the Great Wall, the drone show at Riyue Island Square begins. You can watch the drone show from a VIP perspective on the Great Wall.
After the night tour, go directly to the Duan Family Courtyard or Yushe next to the entrance of the Great Wall to have an open-air hot spring before going to bed. After the end, take a shuttle bus to Wangjing Street to return quickly.
the next day‚Ä¶
In the morning, you can continue to play in the swimming pool after breakfast.
After check-out and check-in luggage to the parking lot, at noon and afternoon, enjoy lunch and coffee in the ancient town relaxedly, wait for the sun to weaken after three o'clock, and then play in the ancient town. There are many projects and many choices, and you can play until the evening before leaving.

If you don‚Äôt want to visit the Great Wall like a special soldier, Gubei Water Town is worth Amway for two days and one night.

msg:After a year, I brought my baby to Gubei Water Town for the second time and chose Hangu Villa Hotel. Three days and two nights, a very satisfying and comfortable vacation experience.
In the late summer and early autumn, the forests are all dyed, the creeks are flowing, and the birds are roaring.

Hangu Villa is located in the Langu area, with 1 to 9 buildings (there seems to be no 4 buildings) built on the mountain. Each building has three floors, and each floor has three guest rooms. There are more than 70 rooms in total, and the room types are all suites of more than 70 square meters. The layout is generally the same (the previous video). The difference between the advanced suite < deluxe < landscape is the floor.
There is a bathtub, a stereo, and a capsule coffee machine. Spare is L'Occitane.

We chose the deluxe suite. The deluxe suite is on the 2nd and some 3rd floors. This balcony faces the south, facing the hill, with floor-to-ceiling windows on three sides.
.
2. The fee includes 3 adults, if the 4 adults are fully occupied, you can add a set of tatami bedding, breakfast, swimming and hot spring tickets if you make up the service fee at the service center.
The tatami in the room can sleep two adults, and the children are particularly novel and like it.

Hot springs and swimming can be reserved on the applet, and hot springs can be selected in Shangcheng (this year, it has been found that the layout has been changed, and the female guest area is much smaller), Yuda and Duanjia.
Swimming In addition to Hangu's own open-air swimming pool, you can also go to Gubeizhiguang (with heating).
.
3. Meals: Breakfast is 80-85 points, the variety is acceptable, and there are basic categories. It is a little less than the light of the ancient north, but after all, the tenants are much less than the light of the north.
Enjoy a cozy brunch outdoors in late summer and early fall.
The restaurant can provide lunch and dinner, but there are not many diners, and there are not many meals that can be ordered, which is slightly expensive.
In the room, a fruit is delivered every morning, and a dessert is delivered in the evening, and the types will be changed.
.
Fourth, the service is very good, the waiters and front desk staff we encountered were very nice. Courteous, thoughtful and warm. The response is relatively timely.
Thumbs up for the management-like staff at the front desk wearing glasses. There is also the waiter who delivered the dessert. The child went out to play and ran into the dining car on the first floor. Although it was not our turn, the lady took the initiative to give the child a small cake in our room in advance.
.
5. The hotel is equipped with an open-air swimming pool and an outdoor children's playground. You can see the drone at the door, and you can walk up the slope for ten minutes to the church and cafe on the top of the mountain.
.
Sixth, the fly in the oin**ent is the inconvenience problem mentioned by many customers.
The shuttle bus from Hangu Hotel can only be sent to the service station at the foot of the mountain. If you go to the water town shuttle bus, you need to cross a bridge and go up a slope to Shanshuicheng Station. If the child does not want to walk and has to be carried, or has a lot of luggage, plus the stone road, I have to say that it is a bit troublesome. (Hint: Luggage can be checked directly from the parking lot to the hotel, or from the hotel to the parking lot)
It is recommended that the water town or hotel find a way to solve this "pain point".

This journey and the weather of more than 30 degrees really made me tired. Because I have been to the water town many times before, I have visited it several times. If it is the first time to come to the water town, it is recommended to stay in a hotel in the central area. During the epidemic period, dine-in is not allowed. The hotel provides two kinds of Chinese food and Western food. The Chinese food includes: shredded pork noodles with pickled vegetables, tomato and egg noodles, two bowls of porridge, pickles, cauliflower, boiled eggs and small buns; Western food includes: milk cereal, small bread, Bacon slices, fried eggs, sausages, green salad, fried mushrooms, and a portion of fruit. The waiter will deliver the meal to the room at the designated time. Personally, I prefer Chinese food. The taste is not bad. The bacon in Western food is too hard. It is suggested that Hangu should coordinate the scenic spot to have a direct shuttle bus for guests who have just checked in, especially in the hot summer.
